## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

# Domain Lineage: Strata FxVanillaOption Type Family Graph

## Your Task

Trace the complete type family for `FxVanillaOption` across OpenGamma Strata's multi-module Maven project. Find: 1. The 4 core Joda-Beans domain classes: `FxVanillaOption`, `FxVanillaOptionTrade`, `ResolvedFxVanillaOption`, `ResolvedFxVanillaOptionTrade` — report each file path under `modules/product/`. 2. The 4 pricer classes (Black, Normal, Vanna-Volga, Implied-Tree variants) under `modules/pricer/` that price these types. 3. The 4 measure calculation classes under `modules/measure/` that wire pricers to the calculation engine. 4. The `FxVanillaOptionTradeCsvPlugin` loader under `modules/loader/`. 5. The `FxSingleBarrierOption` class that embeds `FxVanillaOption` as a dependency. For each file, report the module, path, and class name.

Pricer Classes (modules/pricer/)\n\nFour pricer classes support two pricing methods (Black lognormal model and Vanna-Volga volatility smile model):\n\n1. **BlackFxVanillaOptionTradePricer** (modules/pricer/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/pricer/fxopt/BlackFxVanillaOptionTradePricer.java)\n   - Prices ResolvedFxVanillaOptionTrade using Black (lognormal) model\n   - Delegates product pricing to BlackFxVanillaOptionProductPricer\n   - Implements premium discounting via DiscountingPaymentPricer\n\n2. **BlackFxVanillaOptionProductPricer** (modules/pricer/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/pricer/fxopt/BlackFxVanillaOptionProductPricer.java)\n   - Prices ResolvedFxVanillaOption using Black volatility model\n   - Provides methods for present value, sensitivities (rates, volatility), delta, gamma, vega, theta\n   - Uses DiscountingFxSingleProductPricer for underlying FX component\n\n3. **VannaVolgaFxVanillaOptionTradePricer** (modules/pricer/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/pricer/fxopt/VannaVolgaFxVanillaOptionTradePricer.java)\n   - Prices ResolvedFxVanillaOptionTrade using Vanna-Volga volatility smile model\n   - Delegates to VannaVolgaFxVanillaOptionProductPricer\n   - Handles premium discounting\n\n4. **VannaVolgaFxVanillaOptionProductPricer** (modules/pricer/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/pricer/fxopt/VannaVolgaFxVanillaOptionProductPricer.java)\n   - Prices ResolvedFxVanillaOption using Vanna-Volga volatility smile adjustments\n   - Provides comparable methods to Black pricer (present value, sensitivities)\n   - Uses DiscountingFxSingleProductPricer for FX component\n\n### 3. Measure Calculation Classes (modules/measure/)\n\nFour classes wire the pricers to the calculation engine:\n\n1. **FxVanillaOptionTradeCalculationFunction** (modules/measure/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/measure/fxopt/FxVanillaOptionTradeCalculationFunction.java)\n   - Implements CalculationFunction<FxVanillaOptionTrade>\n   - Wires FxVanillaOptionMeasureCalculations to the calculation engine\n   - Supports measures: PRESENT_VALUE, PV01_CALIBRATED_SUM/BUCKETED, PV01_MARKET_QUOTE_SUM/BUCKETED, CURRENCY_EXPOSURE, OPTION_DELTA, CURRENT_CASH, VEGA_MARKET_QUOTE_BUCKETED\n   - Requires RatesMarketDataLookup and FxOptionMarketDataLookup parameters\n\n2. **FxVanillaOptionMeasureCalculations** (modules/measure/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/measure/fxopt/FxVanillaOptionMeasureCalculations.java)\n   - Internal calculations class using BlackFxVanillaOptionTradePricer and VannaVolgaFxVanillaOptionTradePricer\n   - Implements all scenario-based measure calculations\n   - Routes calculations based on FxVanillaOptionMethod parameter (BLACK or VANNA_VOLGA)\n\n3. **FxVanillaOptionTradeCalculations** (modules/measure/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/measure/fxopt/FxVanillaOptionTradeCalculations.java)\n   - Public API for single-scenario FX vanilla option calculations\n   - Wraps FxVanillaOptionMeasureCalculations\n   - Provides convenience methods for direct calculations on ResolvedFxVanillaOptionTrade\n\n4. **FxVanillaOptionMethod** (modules/measure/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/measure/fxopt/FxVanillaOptionMethod.java)\n   - Enum with two methods: BLACK and VANNA_VOLGA\n   - Implements NamedEnum and CalculationParameter\n   - Acts as the parameter to select which pricer variant to use\n\n### 4. CSV Plugin Loader (modules/loader/)\n\n**FxVanillaOptionTradeCsvPlugin** (modules/loader/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/loader/csv/FxVanillaOptionTradeCsvPlugin.java)\n- Implements TradeCsvParserPlugin and TradeCsvWriterPlugin<FxVanillaOptionTrade>\n- Handles CSV parsing and writing of FxVanillaOptionTrade objects\n- Registered in META-INF configuration files for plugin discovery\n\n### 5. Dependent Type: FxSingleBarrierOption\n\n**FxSingleBarrierOption** (modules/product/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/product/fxopt/FxSingleBarrierOption.java)\n- Embeds FxVanillaOption as its underlying option (property: underlyingOption)\n- Implements FxOptionProduct, Resolvable<ResolvedFxSingleBarrierOption>, ImmutableBean, Serializable\n- Annotated with @BeanDefinition\n- Wraps a vanilla FX option with a barrier condition (knock-in/knock-out)\n- Contains Barrier definition and optional rebate payment\n- Has parallel type hierarchy: ResolvedFxSingleBarrierOption also holds ResolvedFxVanillaOption\n\n## Type Family Hierarchy Summary\n\n```\nFxVanillaOption (unresolved)\n  ↓ resolve(ReferenceData)\nResolvedFxVanillaOption (resolved)\n\nFxVanillaOptionTrade (unresolved)\n  ├─ contains FxVanillaOption product\n  ├─ resolve() → ResolvedFxVanillaOptionTrade\n  └─ FxVanillaOptionMethod.BLACK\n     └─ BlackFxVanillaOptionTradePricer\n        └─ BlackFxVanillaOptionProductPricer\n  └─ FxVanillaOptionMethod.VANNA_VOLGA\n     └─ VannaVolgaFxVanillaOptionTradePricer\n        └─ VannaVolgaFxVanillaOptionProductPricer\n\nResolvedFxVanillaOptionTrade (resolved)\n  ├─ contains ResolvedFxVanillaOption product\n  └─ wired via FxVanillaOptionTradeCalculationFunction\n     └─ FxVanillaOptionMeasureCalculations\n        └─ FxVanillaOptionTradeCalculations\n\nFxSingleBarrierOption (dependent type)\n  └─ contains FxVanillaOption (underlyingOption)\n```\n\nAll found classes are properly annotated with Joda Beans @BeanDefinition for runtime reflection and immutable bean handling. The architecture follows OpenGamma's standard pattern of separating unresolved user-facing types from resolved internal calculation types, with pluggable pricer implementations selected via CalculationParameter enums."
